NOTICE

CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
W ILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
BLUESHIFT INDIA PRIVATE LIMITED
1st Floor, B-WING, 60, LUZ CHURCH ROAD,
MYLAPORE (OPP. NAGESWARA PARK)
CHENNAI-600 004.
True extract of the Minutes of the an EXTRAORDINARY GENERAL MEETING of the company held on 30-11-2015,
at 10.30 AM at 1st Floor, B-Wing, No. 60, Luz Church Road, Mylapore, Chennai-600 004.
Item No. 1.
“RESOLVED THAT having regard to the Declaration of Solvency dated 5th November 2015 made by the Board of
Directors of the Company under section 488 of the Companies Act, 1956, stating that the Company would be able to pay
its debts in full within a period of three years from the date of declaration thereof, the Company, having its Registered Office
at 60, Luz Chruch Road, Mylapore, Chennai-600 004, be wound up voluntarily, pursuant to section 484 (1)(b) of the
Companies Act, 1956.
FURTHER RESOLVED THAT Ms. S. Uma, residing at Old No. 22/3, New No. 59, Venkatakrishna Road, Mandaveli,
Chennai-600 028 be and is hereby appointed as Liquidator of the Company for the purpose of winding up on a remuneration
of Rs. 50,000/-plus out of pocket expenses as actual.
RESOLVED FURTHER THAT Ms. S. Uma, Liquidator of the Company be and is hereby authorized and empowered
to exercise all powers as provided in section 457 of the Companies Act, 1956 and further authorized to file all the necessary
forms, papers, returns, documents etc as may be required, with the Registrar of Companies, Tamil Nadu and/or such other
authorities and/or agency(ies) as may be required, publish, issue any notices, forms advertisements, declarations etc and
to do all such other acts, deeds, matters and things as may be necessary to give effect the forgoing resolution.”

Chennai,
31st December 2015.

K. VENUGOPALAN,
Chairman.

Jan. 6, 2016]

BLUESHIFT INDIA PRIVATE LIMITED
1st Floor, B-Wing, 60, Luz Church Road,
Mylapore (Opp. Nageswara Park)
Chennai-600 004.
Pursuant to section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956, notice is hereby given that at an Extraordinary General Meeting
of the Company held on 30-11-2015 the following Special Resolution was passed unanimously to voluntarily wind up
Blueshift India Private Limited.
RESOLVED THAT having regard to the declaration of solvency dated 5-11-2015 made by the Board of Directors of the
Company under section 488 of the Companies Act, 1956, stating that the Company would be able to pay its debts in full
within a period of three years from the date of declaration thereof, the company, having its Registered Office at 1st Floor,
B-Wing, 60, Luz Church Road, Mylapore (Opp. Nageswara Park), Chennai-600 004 be wound up voluntarily, pursuant to
section 484(1)(b)of the Companies Act, 1956.

Chennai,
31st December 2015.

RADHAKRISHNAN NAMBIAR,
Director.
